 var selectedLocation = '';
 
 var showCompanies = false;
 var filterCompaniesByCountry = true;
 var selectedCompany = '';
 
 var showDivisions = true;
 var filterDivisionsByCountry = false;
 var selectedDivision = '';
 
 function Subject () {
     this.value = "";
   this.observers = new Array();
   this.registerObserver = function(observer){
     this.observers.push(observer);
   }
   this.removeObserver = function(observer){
     for(var i=0; i < this.observers.length; i++){
       if(this.observers[i] === observer){
         this.observers.splice(i, 1);
       }
     }
   }
     this.setValue = function(value){
         this.value = value;
         this.notifyObservers();
     }
     this.notifyObservers  = function(){
     for(var i=0; i < this.observers.length; i++){
             this.observers[i].update(this.value);
       }
     }
 }
   // class for observers
   function Observer(selectId, mappedValues, keyKey, valueKey, allOptions, allInCountryPattern){
     this.allOptions = allOptions;
     this.selectId = selectId;
     this.mappedValues = mappedValues;
     this.keyKey = keyKey;
     this.valueKey = valueKey;
     this.allInCountryPattern = allInCountryPattern;
     countrySubject.registerObserver(this);
     this.update = function(value){
       var country = $("#country").val();
       if (this.mappedValues[country]) {
         clearAndDisableSelectBox(this.selectId);
         var allInCountry = this.allInCountryPattern.replace(/\{0\}/g, $("#country option:selected").text());
         $(this.selectId).append("<option value=\"\" selected=\"selected\">" + allInCountry + "</option>");
         var divMap = this.mappedValues[country];
         for (var key in divMap) {
           $(this.selectId).append("<option value=\"" + divMap[key][this.keyKey] + "\">" + divMap[key][this.valueKey] + "</option>");
         }
         $(this.selectId).removeAttr("disabled");
         if ($(this.selectId).data('stsInitialized') == true)
           $(this.selectId).resetSS();
       }
       else if ($.inArray(country, externalCountryCodes) >= 0) {
     	  clearAndDisableSelectBox(this.selectId, $(eval(allOptions)).first(), true);
       }
       else {
         clearAndDisableSelectBox(this.selectId);
         $(eval(allOptions)).appendTo(this.selectId);
         $(this.selectId).removeAttr("disabled");
         $(this.selectId).children(":first").attr("selected", "selected");
         if ($(this.selectId).data('stsInitialized') == true)
           $(this.selectId).resetSS();
       }
     }
   }
 
   var allLocationsInCountryPattern = "All locations in {0}";
   var allCompaniesInCountryPattern = "All companies in {0}";
   
   var countrySubject = new Subject();
   
   var allAccessLevels = null;
   var allFunkctionalAreas = null;
   var allCountries = null;
   
   var allLocationOptions;
   var locations = { "DE" :{ "0" :{ "LOCATION" :"sap_lo_1059192", "COUNTRY" :"DE", "CC_LOCATION_TXT" :"DE - Bergkamen", "LOCATION_TXT" :"Bergkamen" }, "1" :{ "LOCATION" :"sap_lo_1013353", "COUNTRY" :"DE", "CC_LOCATION_TXT" :"DE -  $(document).ready(function(){
 
     $('#country').on('change', function() {  
         if(this.value === "BR") {
         $('#functional_area').next('div').hide();
          } else {
         $('#functional_area').next('div').show();
         }
     });
 });
 $(window).on("load", function(){
       if ($("#country option:selected").val() === "BR") {
          $('#functional_area').next('div').hide();
     }
 });

       <script>
        function slickCarousel() {
 		$('.clippings-slider').removeClass("slick-initialized slick-slider");
 		$('.clippings-slider').slick({
 			dots: !0,
 			arrows: !1,
 			lazyLoad: "progressive",
 			infinite: !0,
 			speed: 300,
 			slidesToShow: 1,
 			slidesToScroll: 1,
 			slide: ".social-clipping",
 			autoplay: !0
 		});
 	}
 	
 	const typeDataLocale = "en-US";
 	
 	function socialDateParser(data) {
 		
 		const dateOptions = {
 			year: "numeric", 
 			month: "long",  
 			day: "numeric", 
 			hour: "2-digit", 
 			minute: "2-digit"  
 		}; 
 		
 		var newData = new Date(data);
 		
 		return newData.toLocaleTimeString(typeDataLocale, dateOptions);
 	};
 
 	function socialPostBeautify(post) {
 	
 		if (post.length > 150){
 			post = post.substring(0, 149) + "(...)";
 		} 
 
 		return post.replace(/#([^ ]+)/g, '<b>#$1</b>');
 	};
 	
 	function loadFacebookPosts() {
 	
 		const facebookProfile = "BayerCareer";
 		const facebookmaxPost = "3";
 		const facebookFallowUs = "Follow us";
 		const facebookReadMore = "Read more";
 
 		$.ajax({
 		url: 'https://graph.facebook.com/v2.9/'+facebookProfile+'/posts?access_token=EAAXIld1qK1MBAEd9jeayGpnPfCz0I1LinhvwUNKcSlkS5NZBDsdZBC9OYcW026r25rcA7rMkGIZCVrWtzRLbAxy9YunUqXdafNMK49KlHxoZA3zoNjmgJdsWbwCMZCoVcXdcWkmHL1RPRnL3GfCEZAqZCZCxMFRdZBdoP3ZB4ee7HWaLi35JuOhjWu'
 		}).done(function (response) { 
 		
 		//Remove temporary content for replace them
 		document.getElementById('fbSlider').textContent = '';
 		
 		for (var i = 0; i < facebookmaxPost; i++) {
 
 			const postText = socialPostBeautify(response.data[i].message);
 
 			const date = socialDateParser(response.data[i].created_time.replace("+0000", ""));
 			
 			const facebookURL = "https://www.facebook.com/" + facebookProfile;
 		
 			var post = '<div class="social-clipping social-clipping--facebook">';
 				post += '<div class="social-clipping__channel">';
 				post += '<a href="'+facebookURL+'" class="u-ir icn-facebook" target="_blank">Facebook</a>';
 				post += '<a href="'+facebookURL+'" class="social-clipping__follow-us" target="_blank">'+facebookFallowUs+'</a></div>';
 				post += '<div class="social-clipping__date">' + date + '</div>';
 				post += '<p>' + postText + '</p>';
 				post += '<a href="https://www.facebook.com/'+ response.data[i].id +'" class="readmore" target="_blank">'+facebookReadMore+'</a>';
 				post += '</div>';
 
 			$("#fbSlider").prepend(post);
 		}
 		
 			slickCarousel();
 
 		}).fail(function (error) {
 			console.log(error);
 		})
 	}
 
 	(function(root, factory) {
 
 		if (typeof define === 'function' && define.amd) {
 			define([], factory);
 		} else if (typeof exports === 'object') {
 			module.exports = factory();
 		} else {
 			factory();
 		}
 	}(this, function() {
 
 		function handvarweets(tweets) {
 			$('#twSlider').append(tweets);
 		}
 
 		function getElementsByClassName(node, classname) {
 			var ElemArray = [];
 			var regex = new RegExp('(^| )' + classname + '( |$)');
 			var elems = node.getElementsByTagName('*');
 			
 			for (var i = 0, j = elems.length; i < j; i++) {
 				if (regex.test(elems[i].className)) {
 					ElemArray.push(elems[i]);
 				}
 			}
 			return ElemArray;
 		}
 		
 		var twitterProfile = "Bayer";
 		var twittermaxTweets = "3";
 		var twitterFallowUs = "Follow us";
 		var twitterReadMore = "Read more";
 
 		var loadTweets = {
 			fetch: function() {
 			
 				var TwitterScript = null;
 				
 				var head = document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0];
 				
 				if (TwitterScript !== null) {
 					head.removeChild(TwitterScript);
 				}
 				
 				TwitterScript = document.createElement('script');
 				TwitterScript.type = 'text/javascript';						
 				
 				TwitterScript.src = 'https://syndication.twitter.com/timeline/profile?callback=__twttrf.callback&dnt=false&screen_name=' + twitterProfile + '&suppress_response_codes=true&lang=' + $('html').attr('lang') + '&rnd=' + Math.random();
 				
 				try {
 				head.appendChild(TwitterScript);
 				}catch(err) {
 					console.log("FF private mode");
 				}
 				
 			},
 			callback: function(data) {
 				if (data === undefined || data.body === undefined) {
 					return;
 				}
 
 				var div = document.createElement('div');
 				div.innerHTML = data.body;					
 
 				var tweets = [];
 				var times = [];
 				var tids = [];
 				
 				var tmp = div.getElementsByClassName('timeline-Tweet');
 				
 				for(var index = 0; index < twittermaxTweets; index++) {
 					tweets.push(tmp[index].getElementsByClassName('timeline-Tweet-text')[0]);
 					tids.push(tmp[index].getAttribute('data-tweet-id'));
 					times.push(tmp[index].getElementsByClassName('dt-updated')[0]);
 				}
 				
 				if (tweets.length > twittermaxTweets) {
 					tweets.splice(twittermaxTweets, (tweets.length - twittermaxTweets));
 					times.splice(twittermaxTweets, (times.length - twittermaxTweets));
 				}
 				
 				var twitterUrl = 'https://twitter.com/'+ twitterProfile;
 				
 				//Remove temporary content for replace them
 				document.getElementById('twSlider').textContent = '';
 				
 				var op = '';
 				
 				for(var currentTwitt = 0; currentTwitt < twittermaxTweets; currentTwitt++) {
 
 					if (tweets[currentTwitt].textContent) {
 					
 						var postText = socialPostBeautify(tweets[currentTwitt].textContent);
 
 						var date = times[currentTwitt].title;
 						
 						//remove "posted at" string
 						date = date.substring(date.indexOf(":") + 1);
 						
 						//remove time location
 						date = date.split('(')[0];
 						
 						//remove seconds
 						date = date.substring(0, date.indexOf(":") + 3);
 						
 						//Parsing timing for specific date locale
 						if(typeDataLocale === "en-US") {
 							var time = date.substr(date.length - 5);
 							var hours = time.split(':')[0];
 							hours = (hours >= 12) ? " PM" : " AM";
 							date += hours;
 						}
 						
 						op += '<div class="social-clipping social-clipping--twitter">';
 						op += '<div class="social-clipping__channel"><a href="'+twitterUrl+'" class="u-ir icn-twitter" target="_blank">Twitter</a> <a href="'+twitterUrl+'" class="social-clipping__follow-us" target="_blank">'+twitterFallowUs+'</a></div>';
 						op += '<div class="social-clipping__date">' + date + '</div>';
 						op += '<p>' + postText + '</p>';
 						op += '<a href="'+ twitterUrl +'/status/' + tids[currentTwitt] + '" class="readmore" target="_blank">'+twitterReadMore+'</a>';
 						op += '</div>';
 						
 					}
 					
 				}
 				
 				handvarweets(op);
 				slickCarousel();
 			}
 		};
 		
 		window.__twttrf = loadTweets;
 		window.loadTweets = loadTweets;
 		return loadTweets;			
 	}));
 
 	function retry(isDone, next) {
 		var current_trial = 0,
 			max_retry = 50,
 			interval = 10,
 			is_timeout = false;
 		var id = window.setInterval(
 			function() {
 				if (isDone()) {
 					window.clearInterval(id);
 					next(is_timeout);
 				}
 				if (current_trial++ > max_retry) {
 					window.clearInterval(id);
 					is_timeout = true;
 					next(is_timeout);
 				}
 			},
 			10
 		);
 	}
 	
 	function detectPrivateMode(callback) {
 		var is_private;
 	
 		if (window.indexedDB && /Firefox/.test(window.navigator.userAgent)) {
 			var db;
 			try {
 				db = window.indexedDB.open('test');
 			} catch (e) {
 				is_private = true;
 			}
 	
 			if (typeof is_private === 'undefined') {
 				retry(
 					function isDone() {
 						return db.readyState === 'done' ? true : false;
 					},
 					function next(is_timeout) {
 						if (!is_timeout) {
 							is_private = db.result ? false : true;
 						}
 					}
 				);
 			}
 		}  	
 		retry(
 			function isDone() {
 				return typeof is_private !== 'undefined' ? true : false;
 			},
 			function next(is_timeout) {
 				callback(is_private);
 			}
 		);
 	}
 	
 	function loadSocialsPosts() {
 		loadTweets.fetch();
 		loadFacebookPosts();
 	}
 	
 	if (window.indexedDB && /Firefox/.test(window.navigator.userAgent)) {
 		detectPrivateMode(
 			function(is_private) {
 				
 				if(typeof is_private === 'undefined') {
 					return;
 				} else if (is_private) {
 					var facebookPrivateMode = "Visit our profile on Facebook!";
 					var twitterPrivateMode = "Visit our profile on Twitter!";
 					document.getElementById('fbFFslider').innerHTML = facebookPrivateMode;
 					document.getElementById('twFFslider').innerHTML = twitterPrivateMode;
 				} else {
 					loadSocialsPosts();
 				} 
 			}
 		);
 	} else {
 		loadSocialsPosts();
 	};
       </script>
       <div class="section section--1177">

         Discover More
